* [Google 翻译](https://translate.google.cn/#en/zh-CN/RESOLVING%20NAMING%20CONFLICTS%20ON%20WINDOWS%0AWhen%20using%20the%20Command%20Prompt%20on%20Windows%2C%20the%20default%20configuration%20file%20name%20can%20cause%20a%20conflict%20with%20the%20truffle%20executable%2C%20and%20so%20you%20may%20not%20be%20able%20to%20run%20Truffle%20commands%20properly%20on%20existing%20projects.%0A%0AThis%20is%20because%20of%20the%20way%20that%20command%20precedence%20works%20on%20the%20Command%20Prompt.%20The%20truffle.cmd%20executable%20is%20on%20the%20path%20as%20part%20of%20the%20npm%20package%2C%20but%20the%20truffle.js%20configuration%20file%20is%20in%20the%20actual%20directory%20where%20the%20truffle%20command%20is%20run.%20Because%20.js%20is%20an%20acceptable%20executable%20extension%20by%20default%2C%20truffle.js%20takes%20precedence%20over%20truffle.cmd%2C%20causing%20unexpected%20results.%0A%0AAny%20of%20the%20following%20solutions%20will%20remedy%20this%20issue%3A%0A%0ACall%20the%20executable%20file%20explicitly%20using%20its%20.cmd%20extension%20(truffle.cmd%20compile)%0AEdit%20the%20system%20PATHEXT%20environment%20variable%20and%20remove%20.JS%3B%20from%20the%20list%20of%20executable%20extensions%0ARename%20truffle.js%20to%20something%20else%20(truffle-config.js)%0AUse%20Windows%20PowerShell%20or%20Git%20BASH%2C%20as%20these%20shells%20do%20not%20have%20this%20conflict.)

* [Google 翻译](https://translate.google.cn/#en/zh-CN/RESOLVING%20NAMING%20CONFLICTS%20ON%20WINDOWS%0AWhen%20using%20the%20Command%20Prompt%20on%20Windows%2C%20the%20default%20configuration%20file%20name%20can%20cause%20a%20conflict%20with%20the%20truffle%20executable%2C%20and%20so%20you%20may%20not%20be%20able%20to%20run%20Truffle%20commands%20properly%20on%20existing%20projects.%0A%0AThis%20is%20because%20of%20the%20way%20that%20command%20precedence%20works%20on%20the%20Command%20Prompt.%20The%20truffle.cmd%20executable%20is%20on%20the%20path%20as%20part%20of%20the%20npm%20package%2C%20but%20the%20truffle.js%20configuration%20file%20is%20in%20the%20actual%20directory%20where%20the%20truffle%20command%20is%20run.%20Because%20.js%20is%20an%20acceptable%20executable%20extension%20by%20default%2C%20truffle.js%20takes%20precedence%20over%20truffle.cmd%2C%20causing%20unexpected%20results.%0A%0AAny%20of%20the%20following%20solutions%20will%20remedy%20this%20issue%3A%0A%0ACall%20the%20executable%20file%20explicitly%20using%20its%20.cmd%20extension%20(truffle.cmd%20compile)%0AEdit%20the%20system%20PATHEXT%20environment%20variable%20and%20remove%20.JS%3B%20from%20the%20list%20of%20executable%20extensions%0ARename%20truffle.js%20to%20something%20else%20(truffle-config.js)%0AUse%20Windows%20PowerShell%20or%20Git%20BASH%2C%20as%20these%20shells%20do%20not%20have%20this%20conflict.)
